SELECT DISTINCT ?label ?href ?rel ?contentType ?format ?explored ?relevance ?associatedFeed WHERE { 

	GRAPH ?g { 
	  ?link a nm:Link ;
	  nm:explored "false" . 
	   OPTIONAL { ?link nm:associatedFeed ?associatedFeed . } 
		OPTIONAL { ?link nm:label ?label . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:href ?href . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:rel ?rel . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:responseCode ?responseCode . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:contentType ?contentType . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:format ?format . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
    } 
}

SELECT DISTINCT ?feedTitle ?feedHtml ?feedUrl ?entry ?title ?content ?date ?author ?authorHomepage 
WHERE { 

GRAPH ?g { 
   ?entry a schema:article . 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?feedUrl dcterms:title ?feedTitle . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?source nm:htmlUrl ?feedHtml . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:title ?title . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:date ?date . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry schema:articleBody ?content . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:name ?author] . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:homepage ?authorHomepage] . } 
      # admin 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:favourite ?favourite . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:read ?read . } 
   }
} 
ORDER BY DESC(?date) 
LIMIT 100 
OFFSET 0

12:31:56 INFO  [73]   Host                 localhost:3030
12:31:56 INFO  [73]   Accept               sparql-results+xml;charset=UTF-8
12:31:56 INFO  [73]   Accept-Language      en-US,en;q=0.5
12:31:56 INFO  [73]   Connection           keep-alive
12:31:56 INFO  [73]   Referer              http://localhost:8080/river.html
12:31:56 INFO  [73]   User-Agent           Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Ubuntu; Linux i686; rv:30.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/30.0
12:31:56 INFO  [73]   Cache-Control        max-age=0
12:31:56 INFO  [73]   Origin               http://localhost:8080
12:31:56 INFO  [73]   Accept-Encoding      gzip, deflate
12:31:56 INFO  [73] Query = 
PREFIX rss: <http://purl.org/rss/1.0/> 
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> 
PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> 
PREFIX schema: <http://schema.org/> 
PREFIX nm: <http://purl.org/stuff/newsmonitor/> 

SELECT DISTINCT ?feedTitle ?feedHtml ?feedUrl ?entry ?title ?content ?date ?author ?authorHomepage 
WHERE { 

GRAPH ?g { 
   ?entry a schema:article . 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?feedUrl dcterms:title ?feedTitle . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?source nm:htmlUrl ?feedHtml . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:title ?title . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:date ?date . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry schema:articleBody ?content . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:name ?author] . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:homepage ?authorHomepage] . } 
      # admin 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:favourite ?favourite . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:read ?read . } 
   }
} 
ORDER BY DESC(?date) 
LIMIT 100 
OFFSET 0

SELECT DISTINCT ?label ?href ?rel ?contentType ?format ?explored ?relevance ?associatedFeed WHERE { 

	GRAPH ?g { 
	  ?link a nm:Link ;
	  nm:explored "false" . 
	   OPTIONAL { ?link nm:associatedFeed ?associatedFeed . } 
		OPTIONAL { ?link nm:label ?label . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:href ?href . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:rel ?rel . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:responseCode ?responseCode . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:contentType ?contentType . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:format ?format . } 
	    OPTIONAL { ?link nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
    } 
}

SELECT DISTINCT ?feedTitle ?feedHtml ?feedUrl ?entry ?title ?content ?date ?author ?authorHomepage 
WHERE { 

GRAPH ?g { 
   ?entry a schema:article . 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?feedUrl dcterms:title ?feedTitle . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?source nm:htmlUrl ?feedHtml . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:title ?title . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:date ?date . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry schema:articleBody ?content . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:name ?author] . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:homepage ?authorHomepage] . } 
      # admin 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:favourite ?favourite . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:read ?read . } 
   }
} 
ORDER BY DESC(?date) 
LIMIT 100 
OFFSET 0

12:32:13 INFO  [92] Query = 
PREFIX rss: <http://purl.org/rss/1.0/> 
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> 
PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> 
PREFIX schema: <http://schema.org/> 
PREFIX nm: <http://purl.org/stuff/newsmonitor/> 

SELECT DISTINCT ?feedTitle ?feedHtml ?feedUrl ?entry ?title ?content ?date ?author ?authorHomepage 
WHERE { 

GRAPH ?g { 
   ?entry a schema:article . 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?feedUrl dcterms:title ?feedTitle . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?source nm:htmlUrl ?feedHtml . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:title ?title . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:date ?date . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry schema:articleBody ?content . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:name ?author] . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:homepage ?authorHomepage] . } 
      # admin 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:favourite ?favourite . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:read ?read . } 
   }
} 
ORDER BY DESC(?date) 
LIMIT 100 
OFFSET 0

12:33:07 INFO  [132]   Host                 localhost:3030
12:33:07 INFO  [132]   Accept               sparql-results+xml;charset=UTF-8
12:33:07 INFO  [132]   Accept-Language      en-US,en;q=0.8
12:33:07 INFO  [132]   Referer              http://localhost:8080/river.html
12:33:07 INFO  [132]   User-Agent           Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux i686) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/36.0.1985.84 Safari/537.36
12:33:07 INFO  [132]   Connection           keep-alive
12:33:07 INFO  [132]   Accept-Encoding      gzip,deflate,sdch
12:33:07 INFO  [132]   Origin               http://localhost:8080
12:33:07 INFO  [132] Query = 
PREFIX rss: <http://purl.org/rss/1.0/> 
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> 
PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> 
PREFIX schema: <http://schema.org/> 
PREFIX nm: <http://purl.org/stuff/newsmonitor/> 

SELECT DISTINCT ?feedTitle ?feedHtml ?feedUrl ?entry ?title ?content ?date ?author ?authorHomepage 
WHERE { 

GRAPH ?g { 
   ?entry a schema:article . 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?feedUrl dcterms:title ?feedTitle . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?source nm:htmlUrl ?feedHtml . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:title ?title . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:date ?date . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry schema:articleBody ?content . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:name ?author] . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:homepage ?authorHomepage] . } 
      # admin 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:favourite ?favourite . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:read ?read . } 
   }
} 
ORDER BY DESC(?date) 
LIMIT 100 
OFFSET 0

12:33:25 INFO  [150]   Connection           keep-alive

12:33:25 INFO  [150] Query = 
PREFIX rss: <http://purl.org/rss/1.0/> 
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> 
PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> 
PREFIX schema: <http://schema.org/> 
PREFIX nm: <http://purl.org/stuff/newsmonitor/> 

SELECT DISTINCT ?feedTitle ?feedHtml ?feedUrl ?entry ?title ?content ?date ?author ?authorHomepage 
WHERE { 

GRAPH ?g { 
   ?entry a schema:article . 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?feedUrl dcterms:title ?feedTitle . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?source nm:htmlUrl ?feedHtml . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:title ?title . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:date ?date . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry schema:articleBody ?content . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:name ?author] . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:homepage ?authorHomepage] . } 
      # admin 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:favourite ?favourite . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:read ?read . } 
   }
} 
ORDER BY DESC(?date) 
LIMIT 100 
OFFSET 0

12:34:17 INFO  [203] Query = 
PREFIX rss: <http://purl.org/rss/1.0/> 
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> 
PREFIX foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> 
PREFIX schema: <http://schema.org/> 
PREFIX nm: <http://purl.org/stuff/newsmonitor/> 

SELECT DISTINCT ?feedTitle ?feedHtml ?feedUrl ?entry ?title ?content ?date ?author ?authorHomepage 
WHERE { 

GRAPH ?g { 
   ?entry a schema:article . 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?feedUrl dcterms:title ?feedTitle . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { 
         ?source nm:htmlUrl ?feedHtml . 
         ?entry dcterms:source ?feedUrl . 
      } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:title ?title . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:date ?date . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry schema:articleBody ?content . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:name ?author] . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry dcterms:creator [foaf:homepage ?authorHomepage] . } 
      # admin 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:relevance ?relevance . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:favourite ?favourite . } 
      OPTIONAL { ?entry nm:read ?read . } 
   }
} 
ORDER BY DESC(?date) 
LIMIT 100 
OFFSET 0

      OPTIONAL { ?channel nm:responseCode ?responseCode . }

      OPTIONAL { ?channel nm:relevance ?relevance . }
